if (is_file('img/info.png') && (sha1_file('img/info.png') != '2c8d9e0c9fe9a005c7924cc768922003c18ba0bd')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: img/info.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('img/info.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('img/info.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('img/info.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('img/info.png')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): img/info.png');
} else if (sha1_file('img/info.png') != '2c8d9e0c9fe9a005c7924cc768922003c18ba0bd') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): img/info.png');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('img/info.png', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of img/info.png');
}
